'auction_id': auction_id,         'bidder_name': bidder_name,         'bid_amount': bid_amount,         'bid_timestamp': now_str     }     bids.append(new_bid)     write_bids(bids)      # Update auction current_bid     for a in auctions:         if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:             a['current_bid'] = bid_amount             break     write_auctions(auctions)      # Append to bid_history     max_history_id = max((bh['history_id'] for bh in bid_history), default=0)     new_history_id = max_history_id + 1     new_history_entry = {         'history_id': new_history_id,         'auction_id': auction_id,         'auction_name': auction['item_name'],         'bidder_name': bidder_name,         'bid_amount': bid_amount,         'bid_timestamp': now_str     }     bid_history.append(new_history_entry)     write_bid_history(bid_history)      return redirect(url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction_id))   @app.route('/bids') def bid_history():     bids = read_bid_history()     auctions = read_auctions()      # bids: list of dict {bid_id: int, auction_name: str, bidder_name: str, bid_amount: float, bid_timestamp: str}     bids_list = []     for b in bids:         bids_list.append({             'bid_id': b['history_id'],             'auction_name': b['auction_name'],             'bidder_name': b['bidder_name'],             'bid_amount': b['bid_amount'],             'bid_timestamp': b['bid_timestamp']         })      auctions_list = []     for a in auctions:         auctions_list.append({             'auction_id': a['auction_id'],             'item_name': a['item_name']         })      return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids_list, auctions=auctions_list)   @app.route('/categories') def categories():     categories = read_categories()     # categories: list of dict {category_id: int, category_name: str, description: str, item_count: int}     return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)   @app.route('/category/<int:category_id>') def category_items(category_id):     categories = read_categories()     auctions = read_auctions()      category_name = None     for c in categories:         if c['category_id'] == category_id:             category_name = c['category_name']             break     if category_name is None:         return redirect(url_for('auction_catalog'))      filtered_auctions = []     for a in auctions:         if a['category'] == category_name:             filtered_auctions.append({                 'auction_id': a['auction_id'],                 'item_name': a['item_name'],                 'description': a['description'],                 'category': a['category'],                 'current_bid': a['current_bid'],                 'end_time': a['end_time'],                 'image_url': a['image_url']             })      return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, category_name=category_name)   @app.route('/winners') NEED_MODIFY

The backend implementation exhibits the following issues and missing features based on the tests performed:

1. Auctions Loading:
   - Auctions data from 'data/auctions.txt' loads correctly and auctions list contains expected entries.

2. Index Route ('/'):
   - Renders template 'index.html' with auctions data as expected.
   - However, template rendering cannot be fully verified here; test returned auctions count and titles correctly.

3. Bid Route ('/bid'):
   - Only POST method supported. Mandatory GET method to provide minimum_bid is missing.
   - POST route does not handle bid validation:
     * No check if bid_amount is numeric or greater than starting bid.
     * No error message returned on invalid bid.
   - POST route returns the bid info but no confirmation or error.

4. Missing or Incomplete Features:
   - GET /bid should provide information about the minimum bid required.
   - Bid validation such as verifying bid amount is numeric and higher than the starting bid or current highest bid.
   - Error handling for invalid bids with user-friendly messages.
 
Summary:
The backend needs modifications to fully support all expected functionalities including GET /bid route, bid validations, and error messages for invalid bids. Without these, the auction bidding functionality is incomplete and will not work correctly.

Please address these issues and resubmit for testing.
